</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>PROMISSORY NOTE </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(Commercial &#150; Revolving Draw) </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2%; text-indent:-2%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>DATE AND PARTIES. </B>The date of this Promissory
Note (Note) is September&nbsp;22, 2006. The parties and their addresses are: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>LENDER:</B> </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>VALLEY BANK</B> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">36 W. Church Ave. S.W. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Roanoke, Virginia 24011 </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Telephone: (540)&nbsp;342-2265 </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2"><B>BORROWER:</B> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>OPTICAL CABLE CORP</B> </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">a Virginia Corporation </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">5290 Concourse Drive </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Roanoke, Virginia 24019 </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>1.</B> <B>DEFINITIONS. </B>As used in this Note, the terms have the following meanings: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A.</B> <B>Pronouns. </B>The pronouns &#147;I&#148;, &#147;me&#148; and &#147;my&#148; refer to every Borrower signing this Note, individually or together. &#147;You&#148; and &#147;your&#148; refers to the
Loan&#146;s lender. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>B.</B> <B>Note. </B>Note refers to this document, and any extensions, renewals, modifications and substitutions of
this Note. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>C.</B> <B>Loan. </B>Loan refers to this transaction generally, including obligations and duties arising from the terms of all
documents prepared or submitted for this transaction such as applications, security agreements, disclosures or notes, and this Note. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2"><B>D.</B> <B>Loan Documents. </B>Loan Documents refer to all the documents executed as a part of or in connection with the Loan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2"><B>E.</B> <B>Property. </B>Property is any property, real, personal or intangible, that secures my performance of the obligations of this Loan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>F.</B> <B>Percent. </B>Rates and rate change limitations are expressed as annualized percentages. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>2.</B> <B>PROMISE
TO PAY. </B>For value received, I promise to pay you or your order, at your address, or at such other location as you may designate, the lesser of the aggregate unpaid amounts advanced from time to time under the terms of this Note or
<B>$2,000,000.00 (Principal) </B>plus interest from the date of disbursement, on the unpaid outstanding Principal balance until this Note is paid in full and Lender has no further obligations to make advances to you under this Loan. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">I may borrow up to the Principal amount more than one time. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">All advances
made will be made subject to all other terms and conditions of this Loan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>3.</B> <B>INTEREST. </B>Interest will accrue on the unpaid Principal balance
of this Note at the rate of <B>7.54 percent (Interest Rate)</B> until October&nbsp;1, 2006, after which time it may change as described in the Variable Rate subsection. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A.</B> <B>Interest After Default. </B>If a default occurs under the terms of this Loan, including for failure to pay in full at maturity, you may increase the Interest Rate payable on the outstanding Principal
balance of this Note. In such event, interest will accrue on the outstanding Principal balance at the Interest Rate in effect from time to time under the terms of this Loan, until paid in full. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>B.</B> <B>Maximum Interest Amount. </B>Any amount assessed or collected as interest under the terms of the Note will be limited to the maximum lawful
amount of interest allowed by state or federal law, whichever is greater. Amounts collected in excess of the maximum lawful amount will be applied first to the unpaid Principal balance. Any remainder will be refunded to me. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>C.</B> <B>Statutory Authority. </B>The amount assessed or collected on this Note is authorized by the Virginia usury laws under Va. Code &#167;&#167;
6.1-330.49 et. seq. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>D.</B> <B>Accrual. </B>Interest accrues using an Actual/360 days counting method. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>E.</B> <B>Variable Rate. </B>The Interest Rate may change during the term of this transaction. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:8%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>(1) </B>Index. Beginning with the first Change Date, the Interest Rate will be based on the following index: defined as the monthly average of
interbank offered rates for dollar deposits in the London market based on quotations at the five major London banks and which is commonly known as the LIBOR rate (i.e. the London InterBank Offered Rate) as quoted and published in the Wall Street
Journal from time to time. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:8%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Current Index is the most recent index figure available on each Change Date. You do not guaranty by
selecting this Index, or the margin, that the Interest Rate on this Note will be the same rate you charge on any other loans or class of loans you make to me or other borrowers. If this Index is no longer available, you will substitute a similar
index. You will give me notice of your choice. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:8%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>(2) </B>Change Date. Each date on which the Interest Rate may change is called a Change Date. The
Interest Rate may change October&nbsp;1, 2006 and every 30 days thereafter. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:8%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>(3) </B>Calculation Of Change. On each Change Date you will
calculate the Interest Rate, which will be the Current Index plus 2.150 percent. The result of this calculation will be rounded to the nearest .01 percent. Subject to any limitations, this will be the Interest Rate until the next Change Date. The
new Interest Rate will become effective on each Change Date. The Interest Rate and other charges on this Note will never exceed the highest rate or charge allowed by law for this Note. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:8%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>(4) </B>Effect Of Variable Rate. A change in the Interest Rate will have the following effect on the payments: The amount of scheduled payments will
change. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>4.</B> <B>REMEDIAL CHARGES. </B>In addition to interest or other finance charges, I agree that I will pay these additional fees based on my
method and pattern of payment. Additional remedial charges may be described elsewhere in this Note. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A.</B> <B>Late Charge. </B>If a
payment is more than <B>7 </B>days late, I will be charged <B>5.000 </B>percent of the Unpaid Portion of Payment. I will pay this late charge promptly but only once for each late payment. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>B.</B> <B>Returned Check Charge. </B>I agree to pay a fee not to exceed $29.00 for each check, negotiable order of withdrawal or draft I issue in
connection with this Loan that is returned because it has been dishonored. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>5.</B> <B>GOVERNING AGREEMENT. </B>This Note is further governed by the
Commercial Loan Agreement executed between you and me as part of this Loan, as modified, amended or supplemented. The Commercial Loan Agreement states the terms and conditions of this note, including the terms and conditions under which the maturity
of this Note may be accelerated. When I sign this Note, I represent to you that I have reviewed and am in compliance with the terms contained in the Commercial Loan Agreement. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>6.</B> <B>PAYMENT. </B>All unpaid principal, accrued interest, costs and expenses are due and payable on February&nbsp;28, 2008 provided that I shall pay this Note on demand with 60 days prior written notice of
demand. Notwithstanding the foregoing, in the event the Company defaults hereunder or under any other Loan Document you may immediately declare the Loan due and payable in full, together with all other amounts owed hereunder. Upon the effective date
of the demand the entire unpaid balance of Principal and accrued interest, long with any earned, and unpaid fees or charges, and the amount of any advances made on my behalf, will be due and owing. Until demand is made, accrued interest is due and
payable in monthly payments on the 1st of each month beginning October&nbsp;1, 2006, or the day following if the payment day is a holiday or is a non-business day for Bank. Unless paid sooner, all unpaid principal, accrued interest, costs and
expenses are due and payable on demand. If the contract rate changes, any remaining payments may be a different amount. All amounts shall be paid in legal U.S. Currency. Any payment made with a check will constitute payment only when collected.
Payments will be rounded to the nearest $.01. With the final payment I also agree to pay any additional fees or charges owing and the amount of any advances you have made to others on my behalf. Payments scheduled to be paid on the 29th, 30th or
31st day of a month that contains no such day will, instead, be made on the last day of such month. Each payment I make on this Note will be applied first to interest that is due then to principal that is due, and finally to any charges that I owe
other than principal and interest. If you and I agree to a different application of payments, we will describe our agreement on this Note. You may change how payments are applied in your sole discretion without notice to me. The actual amount of my
final payment will depend on my payment record. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>7.</B> <B>PREPAYMENT. </B>I may prepay this Loan in full or in part at any time. Any partial prepayment
will not excuse any later scheduled payments until I pay in full. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>8.</B> <B>LOAN PURPOSE. </B>The purpose of this Loan is to establish a Line Manager
Line of Credit to support working capital. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>9.</B> <B>ADDITIONAL TERMS.</B> This note is cross collateralized and cross defaulted with note numbers
156809&nbsp;&amp; 156779. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>10.</B> <B>SECURITY. </B>This loan is secured by separate security instruments prepared together with this Note as follows:

regardless of the number of such renewals or extensions. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:8%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>(2) </B>You may release any Borrower, endorser, guarantor, surety,

<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:8%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>(4) </B>You, or any institution participating in this Note, may invoke your right of set-off. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:8%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>(5) </B>You may enter into any sales, repurchases or participations of this Note to any person in any
amounts and I waive notice of such sales, repurchases or participations. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:8%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>(6) </B>I agree that any of us signing this Note as a Borrower
is authorized to modify the terms of this Note or any instrument securing, guarantying or relating to this Note. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>B.</B> <B>No Waiver By
Lender. </B>Your course of dealing, or your forbearance from, or delay in, the exercise of any of your rights, remedies, privileges or right to insist upon my strict performance of any provisions contained in this Note, or any other Loan Document,
shall not be construed as a waiver by you, unless any such waiver is in writing and is signed by you. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>13.</B> <B>COMMISSIONS. </B>I understand and
agree that you (or your affiliate) will earn commissions or fees on any insurance products, and may earn such fees on other services that I buy through you or your affiliate. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>14.</B> <B>APPLICABLE LAW. </B>This Note is governed by the laws of Virginia, the United States of America, and to the extent required, by the laws of the jurisdiction where the Property is located, except to the
extent such state laws are preempted by federal law. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>15.</B> <B>JOINT AND INDIVIDUAL LIABILITY AND SUCCESSORS. </B>My obligation to pay the Loan is
independent of the obligation of any other person who has also agreed to pay it. You may sue me alone, or anyone else who is obligated on the Loan, or any number of us together, to collect the Loan. Extending the Loan or new obligations under the
Loan, will not affect my duty under the Loan and I will still be obligated to pay the Loan. This Note shall inure to the benefit of and be enforceable by you and your successors and assigns and shall be binding upon and enforceable against me and my
personal representatives, successors, heirs and assigns. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>16.</B> <B>AMENDMENT, INTEGRATION AND SEVERABILITY. </B>This Note may not be amended or
modified by oral agreement. No amendment or modification of this Note is effective unless made in writing and executed by you and me. This Note and the other Loan Documents are the complete and final expression of the agreement. If any provision of
this Note is unenforceable, then the unenforceable provision will be severed and the remaining provisions will still be enforceable. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>17.</B>
<B>INTERPRETATION. </B>Whenever used, the singular includes the plural and the plural includes the singular. The section headings are for convenience only and are not to be used to interpret or define the terms of this Note. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>18.</B> <B>NOTICE, FINANCIAL REPORTS AND ADDITIONAL DOCUMENTS. </B>Unless otherwise required by law, any notice will be given by delivering it or mailing it by first
class mail to the appropriate party&#146;s address listed in the DATE AND PARTIES section, or to any other address designated in writing. Notice to one Borrower will be deemed to be notice to all Borrowers. I will inform you in writing of any change
in my name, address or other application information. I agree to sign, deliver, and file any additional documents or certifications that you may consider necessary to perfect, continue, and preserve my obligations under this Loan and to confirm your
lien status on any Property. Time is of the essence. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>19.</B> <B>CREDIT INFORMATION. </B>I agree to supply you with whatever information you reasonably
feel you need to decide whether to continue this Loan. You will make requests for this information without undue frequency and will give me reasonable time in which to supply the information. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>20.</B> <B>ERRORS AND OMISSIONS. </B>I agree, if requested by you, to fully cooperate in the correction, if necessary, in the reasonable discretion of you of any and
all loan closing documents so that all documents accurately describe the loan between you and me. I agree to assume all costs including by way of illustration and not limitation, actual expenses, legal fees and marketing losses for failing to
reasonably comply with your requests within thirty (30)&nbsp;days. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>21.</B> <B>SIGNATURES. </B>By signing under seal, I agree to the terms contained in
this Note. I also acknowledge receipt of a copy of this Note. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>BORROWER:</B> </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:13%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Optical Cable Corporation </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Exhibit 4.10 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Space Above This Line For Recording Data </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2%; text-indent:-2%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Parcel Identification Number:
037.07-01-05.02-0000, 037.07-01-15.01-0000, 037.07-01-15.00- 0000 </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2%; text-indent:-2%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">This document was prepared by M. Nelson Metheney,
Valley Bank, 36 W. Church Avenue, S.W., Roanoke, Virginia 24011 </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>THIS IS A CREDIT LINE DEED OF TRUST </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(With Future Advance Clause) </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>DATE AND PARTIES. </B>The
date of this Deed Of Trust (Security Instrument) is September&nbsp;22, 2006. The parties and their addresses are: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>GRANTOR:</B>
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Optical Cable Corporation</B> </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A Virginia Corporation </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">5290 Concourse Drive </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Roanoke, Virginia 24019 </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>TRUSTEE:</B> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>John T.
MCCALEB</B> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">36 W. Church Ave </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Roanoke, Virginia 24011 </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Catherine J HARTMAN</B> </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">36 W. Church Ave </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">Roanoke , Virginia 24011 </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>LENDER:</B> </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>VALLEY BANK</B> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">Organized and existing under the laws of Virginia </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">36 W. Church Ave. S.W. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Roanoke, Virginia 24011 </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>1. CREDIT LINE
DEED OF TRUST. </B>THIS IS A CREDIT LINE DEED OF TRUST within the meaning of Section&nbsp;55-58.2 of the Code of Virginia (1950), as amended. For purposes of such section, (i)&nbsp;the name of the noteholder secured by this Security Instrument is
VALLEY BANK, (ii)&nbsp;the address at which communications may be mailed or delivered to the noteholder is 36 W. Church Ave. S.W., Roanoke, Virginia 24011, and (iii)&nbsp;the maximum aggregate principal amount to be secured is $8,100,000.00.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>2. CONVEYANCE. </B>For good and valuable consideration, the receipt and sufficiency of which is acknowledged, and to secure the Secured Debts and
Grantor&#146;s performance under this Security Instrument, Grantor irrevocably grants, conveys and sells to Trustee, in trust for the benefit of Lender, with power of sale, the following described property: </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2%; text-indent:-2%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">See attached Exhibit &#147;A&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The
property is located in Roanoke County at 5290 Concourse Drive, Roanoke, Virginia 24019. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Together with all rights, easements, appurtenances, royalties,
mineral rights, oil and gas rights, all water and riparian rights, wells, ditches and water stock, crops, timber, all diversion payments or third </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">party payments made to crop producers and all existing and future improvements, structures, fixtures, and replacements
that may now, or at any time in the future, be part of the real estate described (all referred to as Property). This Security Instrument will remain in effect until the Secured Debts and all underlying agreements have been terminated in writing by
Lender. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>3. MAXIMUM OBLIGATION LIMIT. </B>The total principal amount secured by this Security Instrument at any one time will not exceed $8,100,000.00.
This limitation of amount does not include interest and other fees and charges validly made pursuant to this Security Instrument. Also, this limitation does not apply to advances made under the terms of this Security Instrument to protect
Lender&#146;s security and to perform any of the covenants contained in this Security Instrument. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>4. SECURED DEBTS. </B>The term &#147;Secured
Debts&#148; includes and this Security Instrument will secure each of the following: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A. Specific Debts. </B>The following debts and all
extensions, renewals, refinancings, modifications and replacements. A promissory note or other agreement, No.&nbsp;156779 , dated September&nbsp;22, 2006, from Grantor to Lender, with a loan amount of $6,500,000.00, with an interest rate of 7.5
percent per year until October&nbsp;1, 2007, then with an interest rate of 7.500 percent per year and maturing on October&nbsp;1, 2011. Promissory note #156809, dated September&nbsp;22, 2006 in the name of Optical Cable Corporation in the amount of
$5,000,000. Promissory note #156833, dated September&nbsp;22, 2006 in the name of Optical Cable Corporation, in the amount of $2,000,000. One or more of the debts secured by this Security Instrument contains a future advance provision. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>B. All Debts. </B>All present and future debts from Grantor to Lender, even if this Security Instrument is not specifically referenced, or if the
future debt is unrelated to or of a different type than this debt. If more than one person signs this Security Instrument, each agrees that it will secure debts incurred either individually or with others who may not sign this Security Instrument.
Nothing in this Security Instrument constitutes a commitment to make additional or future loans or advances. Any such commitment must be in writing. In the event that Lender fails to provide any required notice of the right of rescission, Lender
waives any subsequent security interest in the Grantor&#146;s principal dwelling that is created by this Security Instrument. This Security Instrument will not secure any debt for which a non-possessory, non-purchase money security interest is
created in &#147;household goods&#148; in connection with a &#147;consumer loan,&#148; as those terms are defined by federal law governing unfair and deceptive credit practices. This Security Instrument will not secure any debt for which a security
interest is created in &#147;margin stock&#148; and Lender does not obtain a &#147;statement of purpose,&#148; as defined and required by federal law governing securities. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>C. Sums Advanced. </B>All sums advanced and expenses incurred by Lender under the terms of this Security Instrument. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2"><B>5. PAYMENTS. </B>Grantor agrees that all payments under the Secured Debts will be paid when due and in accordance with the terms of the Secured Debts and this Security Instrument. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>6. WARRANTY OF TITLE. </B>Grantor warrants that Grantor is or will be lawfully seized of the estate conveyed by this Security Instrument and has the right to
irrevocably grant, convey and sell the Property to Trustee, in trust, with power of sale. Grantor also warrants that the Property is unencumbered, except for encumbrances of record. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>7. PRIOR SECURITY INTERESTS. </B>With regard to any other mortgage, deed of trust, security agreement or other lien document that created a prior security interest or encumbrance on the Property, Grantor agrees:
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A. </B>To make all payments when due and to perform or comply with all covenants. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>B. </B>To promptly deliver to Lender any notices that Grantor receives from the holder. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>C. </B>Not to allow any modification or extension of, nor to request any future advances under any note or agreement secured by the lien document
without Lender&#146;s prior written consent. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>8. CLAIMS AGAINST TITLE. </B>Grantor will pay all taxes, assessments, liens, encumbrances, lease payments,
ground rents, utilities, and other charges relating to the Property when due, except for immaterial liens related to claims being contested by Grantor. Lender may require Grantor to provide to Lender copies of all notices </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">that such amounts are due and the receipts evidencing Grantor&#146;s payment. Grantor will defend title to the Property
against any claims that would impair the lien of this Security Instrument. Grantor agrees to assign to Lender, as requested by Lender, any rights, claims or defenses Grantor may have against parties who supply labor or materials to maintain or
improve the Property. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>9. DUE ON SALE OR ENCUMBRANCE. </B>Lender may, at its option, declare the entire balance of the Secured Debt to be immediately
due and payable upon the creation of, or contract for the creation of, any lien, encumbrance, transfer or sale of all or any part of the Property, except for immaterial liens related to claims being contested by Grantor. This right is subject to the
restrictions imposed by federal law (12 C.F.R. 591), as applicable. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>10. WARRANTIES AND REPRESENTATIONS. </B>Grantor makes to Lender the following
warranties and representations which will continue as long as this Security Instrument is in effect: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A. Power. </B>Grantor is duly
organized, and validly existing and in good standing in all jurisdictions in which Grantor operates. Grantor has the power and authority to enter into this transaction and to carry on Grantor&#146;s business or activity as it is now being conducted
and, as applicable, is qualified to do so in each jurisdiction in which Grantor operates. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>B. Authority. </B>The execution, delivery and
performance of this Security Instrument and the obligation evidenced by this Security Instrument are within Grantor&#146;s powers, have been duly authorized, have received all necessary governmental approval, will not violate any provision of law,
or order of court or governmental agency, and will not violate any agreement to which Grantor is a party or to which Grantor is or any of Grantor&#146;s property is subject. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>C. Name and Place of Business. </B>Other than previously disclosed in writing to Lender, Grantor has not changed Grantor&#146;s name or principal place
of business within the last 5 years and has not used any other trade or fictitious name. Without Lender&#146;s prior written consent, Grantor does not and will not use any other name and will preserve Grantor&#146;s existing name, trade names and
franchises. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>11. PROPERTY CONDITION, ALTERATIONS AND INSPECTION. </B>Grantor will keep the Property in good condition and make all repairs that are
reasonably necessary. Grantor will not commit or allow any waste, impairment, or deterioration of the Property. Grantor will keep the Property free of noxious weeds and grasses. Grantor agrees that the nature of the occupancy and use will not
substantially change without Lender&#146;s prior written consent. Grantor will not permit any change in any license, restrictive covenant or easement without Lender&#146;s prior written consent. Grantor will notify Lender of all demands,
proceedings, claims, and actions against Grantor, and of any loss or damage to the Property. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">No portion of the Property will be removed, demolished or
materially altered without Lender&#146;s prior written consent except that Grantor has the right to remove items of personal property comprising a part of the Property that become worn or obsolete, provided that such personal property is replaced
with other personal property at least equal in value to the replaced personal property, free from any title retention device, security agreement or other encumbrance. Such replacement of personal property will be deemed subject to the security
interest created by this Security Instrument. Grantor will not partition or subdivide the Property without Lender&#146;s prior written consent. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Lender or
Lender&#146;s agents may, at Lender&#146;s option, enter the Property at any reasonable time for the purpose of inspecting the Property. Lender will give Grantor notice at the time of or before an inspection specifying a reasonable purpose for the
inspection. Any inspection of the Property will be entirely for Lender&#146;s benefit and Grantor will in no way rely on Lender&#146;s inspection. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>12.
AUTHORITY TO PERFORM. </B>If Grantor fails to perform any duty or any of the covenants contained in this Security Instrument, Lender may, without notice, perform or cause them to be performed. Grantor appoints Lender as attorney in fact to sign
Grantor&#146;s name or pay any amount necessary for performance. Lender&#146;s right to perform for Grantor will not create an obligation to perform, and Lender&#146;s failure to perform will not preclude Lender from exercising any of Lender&#146;s
other rights under the law or this Security Instrument. If any construction on the Property is discontinued or not carried on in a reasonable manner, Lender may take all steps necessary to protect Lender&#146;s security interest in the Property,
including completion of the construction. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>13. DEFAULT. </B>Grantor will be in default if any of the following occur: </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A. Payments. </B>Grantor fails to make a payment in full within five days of when due. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>B. Insolvency or Bankruptcy. </B>The death, dissolution or insolvency of, appointment of a receiver by or on behalf of, application of any debtor
relief law, the assignment for the benefit of creditors by or on behalf of, the voluntary or involuntary termination of existence by, or the commencement of any proceeding under any present or future federal or state insolvency, bankruptcy,
reorganization, composition or debtor relief law by or against Grantor, Borrower, or any co-signer, endorser, surety or guarantor of this Security Instrument or any other obligations Borrower has with Lender. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>C. Business Termination. </B>Grantor merges, dissolves, reorganizes, ends its business or existence, or a partner or majority owner dies or is declared
legally incompetent. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>D. Failure to Perform. </B>Grantor fails to perform any condition or to keep any promise or covenant of this
Security Instrument. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>E. Other Documents. </B>A default occurs under the terms of any other document relating to the Secured Debts.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>F. Other Agreements. </B>Grantor is in default on any other debt or agreement Grantor has with Lender. <B> </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>G. Misrepresentation. </B>Grantor makes any verbal or written statement or provides any financial information that is untrue, inaccurate, or conceals a
material fact at the time it is made or provided. <B> </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>H. Judgment. </B>Grantor fails to satisfy or appeal any judgment in excess of
$50,000 against Grantor. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>I. Forfeiture. </B>The Property is used in a manner or for a purpose that threatens confiscation by a legal
authority. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>J. Name Change. </B>Grantor changes Grantor&#146;s name or assumes an additional name without notifying Lender before making
such a change. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>K. Property Transfer. </B>Grantor transfers all or a substantial part of Grantor&#146;s money or property. This condition
of default, as it relates to the transfer of the Property, is subject to the restrictions Contained in the DUE ON SALE section. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>L.
Property Value. </B>Lender determines in good faith that the value of the Property has materially declined or is materially impaired. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>M.
Material Change. </B>Without first notifying Lender, there is a material change in Grantor&#146;s business, including ownership, management, and financial conditions. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>N. Insecurity. </B>Lender determines in good faith that a material adverse change has occurred in Grantor&#146;s financial condition from the conditions set forth in Grantor&#146;s most recent financial statement
before the date of this Security Instrument or that the prospect for payment or performance of the Secured Debts is materially impaired for any reason. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2"><B>14. REMEDIES. </B>On or after default, Lender may use any and all remedies Lender has under state or federal law or in any document relating to the Secured Debts. Any amounts advanced on Grantor&#146;s behalf will be immediately due and
may be added to the balance owing under the Secured Debts. Lender may make a claim for any and all insurance benefits or refunds that may be available on Grantor&#146;s default. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Subject to any right to cure, required time schedules or any other notice rights Grantor may have under federal and state law, Lender may make all or any part of the amount owing by the terms of the Secured Debts
immediately due and foreclose this Security Instrument in a manner provided by law upon the occurrence of a default or anytime thereafter. In addition to these remedies, Lender has, without limitation, the power to direct the Trustee to execute the
trust created hereby and in so doing exercise all of the powers under applicable law and as set forth in Va. Code Section&nbsp;55-59 and 55-59.1 through 55-59.4, as in effect on the date of this Security Instrument. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If there is a default, Trustee will, in addition to any other permitted remedy, at the request of the Lender, advertise
and sell the Property as a whole or in separate parcels at public auction to the highest bidder for cash. Trustee will give notice of sale including the time, terms and place of sale and a description of the Property to be sold as required by the
applicable law in effect at the time of the proposed sale. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Advertisement required: Advertisement shall be sufficient if published in a newspaper having a
general circulation in the County or City where the Property or some part thereof is located either (a)&nbsp;once a week for two weeks, or (b)&nbsp;once a day for three days, which may be consecutive days. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Upon sale of the Property, Trustee shall apply the proceeds in the order prescribed by law. Lender may purchase the Property. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Upon any sale of the Property, Trustee will make and deliver a special or limited warranty deed that conveys the property sold to the purchaser or purchasers. Under this
special or limited warranty deed, Trustee will covenant that Trustee has not caused or allowed a lien or an encumbrance to burden the Property and that Trustee will specially warrant and defend the Property&#146;s title of the purchaser or
purchasers at the sale against all lawful claims and demand of all persons claiming by, through or under Trustee. The recitals in any deed of conveyance will be prima facie evidence of the facts set forth therein. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">All remedies are distinct, cumulative and not exclusive, and the Lender is entitled to all remedies provided at law or equity, whether or not expressly set forth. The
acceptance by Lender of any sum in payment or partial payment on the Secured Debts after the balance is due or is accelerated or after foreclosure proceedings are filed will not constitute a waiver of Lender&#146;s right to require full and complete
cure of any existing default. By not exercising any remedy, Lender does not waive Lender&#146;s right to later consider the event a default if it continues or happens again. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>15. SECTION 55-60 OF THE CODE OF VIRGINIA. </B>This Security Instrument will be construed to impose and confer upon the parties hereto, and the beneficiaries hereunder, all duties, rights and obligations prescribed
in Section&nbsp;55-60 of the Code of Virginia (1950), as amended, and in effect on the date of this Security Instrument, and the following provisions of that section are incorporated in this Security Instrument by short form reference: </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A. </B>Exemptions waived. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>B.
</B>Subject to all upon default. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>C. </B>Renewal, extension or reinstatement permitted. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>D. </B>Any Trustee may act. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>E.
</B>Substitution of Trustees permitted. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>16. COLLECTION EXPENSES AND ATTORNEYS&#146; FEES. </B>On or after Default, to the extent permitted by law,
Grantor agrees to pay all expenses of collection, enforcement or protection of Lender&#146;s rights and remedies under this Security Instrument or any other document relating to the Secured Debts. Grantor agrees to pay expenses for Lender to inspect
and preserve the Property and for any recordation costs of releasing the Property from this Security Instrument. Expenses include (unless prohibited by law) reasonable attorneys&#146; fees, court costs, and other legal expenses. These expenses are
due and payable immediately. If not paid immediately, these expenses will bear interest from the date of payment until paid in full at the highest interest rate in effect as provided for in the terms of the Secured Debts. In addition, to the extent
permitted by the United States Bankruptcy Code, Grantor agrees to pay the reasonable attorneys&#146; fees incurred by Lender to protect Lender&#146;s rights and interests in connection with any bankruptcy proceedings initiated by or against Grantor.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>17. ENVIRONMENTAL LAWS AND HAZARDOUS SUBSTANCES. </B>As used in this section, (1)&nbsp;Environmental Law means, without limitation, the Comprehensive
Environmental Response, Compensation and Liability Act (CERCLA, 42 U.S.C. 9601 et seq.), all other federal, state and local laws, regulations, ordinances, court orders, attorney general opinions or interpretive letters concerning the public health,
safety, welfare, environment or a hazardous substance; and (2)&nbsp;Hazardous Substance means any toxic, radioactive or hazardous material, waste, pollutant or contaminant which has </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">characteristics which render the substance dangerous or potentially dangerous to the public health, safety, welfare or
environment. The term includes, without limitation, any substances defined as &#147;hazardous material,&#148; &#147;toxic substance,&#148; &#147;hazardous waste,&#148; &#147;hazardous substance,&#148; or &#147;regulated substance&#148; under any
Environmental Law. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2%; text-indent:-2%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Grantor represents, warrants and agrees that: </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A. </B>Except as previously disclosed and acknowledged in writing to Lender, no Hazardous Substance has been, is, or will be located, transported,
manufactured, treated, refined, or handled by any person on, under or about the Property, except in the ordinary course of business and in strict compliance with all applicable Environmental Law. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>B. </B>Except as previously disclosed and acknowledged in writing to Lender, Grantor has not and will not cause, contribute to, or permit the release
of any Hazardous Substance on the Property. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>C. </B>Grantor will immediately notify Lender if (1)&nbsp;a release or threatened release of
Hazardous Substance occurs on, under or about the Property or migrates or threatens to migrate from nearby property; or (2)&nbsp;there is a violation of any Environmental Law concerning the Property. In such an event, Grantor will take all necessary
remedial action in accordance with Environmental Law. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>D. </B>Except as previously disclosed and acknowledged in writing to Lender,
Grantor has no knowledge of or reason to believe there is any pending or threatened investigation, claim, or proceeding of any kind relating to (1)&nbsp;any Hazardous Substance located on, under or about the Property; or (2)&nbsp;any violation by
Grantor or any tenant of any Environmental Law. Grantor will immediately notify Lender in writing as soon as Grantor has reason to believe there is any such pending or threatened investigation, claim, or proceeding. In such an event, Lender has the
right, but not the obligation, to participate in any such proceeding including the right to receive copies of any documents relating to such proceedings. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>E. </B>Except as previously disclosed and acknowledged in writing to Lender, Grantor and every tenant have been, are and will remain in full compliance with any applicable Environmental Law. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>F. </B>Except as previously disclosed and acknowledged in writing to Lender, there are no underground storage tanks, private dumps or open wells
located on or under the Property and no such tank, dump or well will be added unless Lender first consents in writing. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>G. </B>Grantor
will regularly inspect the Property, monitor the activities and operations on the Property, and confirm that all permits, licenses or approvals required by any applicable Environmental Law are obtained and complied with. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>H. </B>Grantor will permit, or cause any tenant to permit, Lender or Lender&#146;s agent to enter and inspect the Property and review all records at
any reasonable time to determine (1)&nbsp;the existence, location and nature of any Hazardous Substance on, under or about the Property; (2)&nbsp;the existence, location, nature, and magnitude of any Hazardous Substance that has been released on,
under or about the Property; or (3)&nbsp;whether or not Grantor and any tenant are in compliance with applicable Environmental Law. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>I.
</B>Upon Lender&#146;s request with a reasonable basis and at any time, Grantor agrees, at Grantor&#146;s expense, to engage a qualified environmental engineer to prepare an environmental audit of the Property and to submit the results of such audit
to Lender. The choice of the environmental engineer who will perform such audit is subject to Lender&#146;s approval. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>J. </B>Lender has
the right, but not the obligation, to perform any of Grantor&#146;s obligations under this section at Grantor&#146;s expense. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>K. </B>As
a consequence of any breach of any representation, warranty or promise made in this section, (1)&nbsp;Grantor will indemnify and hold Lender and Lender&#146;s successors or assigns harmless from and against all losses, claims, demands, liabilities,
damages, cleanup, response and remediation costs, penalties and expenses, including without limitation all costs of litigation and attorneys&#146; fees, which Lender and Lender&#146;s successors or assigns may sustain; and (2)&nbsp;at Lender&#146;s
discretion, Lender may release this Security Instrument and in return Grantor will provide Lender with collateral of at least equal value to the Property without prejudice to any of Lender&#146;s rights under this Security Instrument. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>L. </B>Notwithstanding any of the language contained in this Security Instrument to the contrary, the
terms of this section will survive any foreclosure or satisfaction of this Security Instrument regardless of any passage of title to Lender or any disposition by Lender of any or all of the Property. Any claims and defenses to the contrary are
hereby waived. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>18. CONDEMNATION. </B>Grantor will give Lender prompt notice of any pending or threatened action by private or public entities to
purchase or take any or all of the Property through condemnation, eminent domain, or any other means. Grantor authorizes Lender to intervene in Grantor&#146;s name in any of the above described actions or claims. Grantor assigns to Lender the
proceeds of any award or claim for damages connected with a condemnation or other taking of all or any part of the Property. Such proceeds will be considered payments and will be applied as provided in this Security Instrument. This assignment of
proceeds is subject to the terms of any prior mortgage, deed of trust, security agreement or other lien document. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>19. INSURANCE. </B>Grantor agrees to
keep the Property insured against the risks reasonably associated with the Property. Grantor will maintain this insurance in the amounts Lender reasonably requires. This insurance will last until the Property is released from this Security
Instrument. What Lender requires pursuant to the preceding two sentences can change during the term of the Secured Debts. Grantor may choose the insurance company, subject to Lender&#146;s approval, which will not be unreasonably withheld.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">All insurance policies and renewals will include a standard &#147;mortgage clause&#148; and, where applicable, &#147;loss payee clause.&#148; If required
by Lender, Grantor agrees to maintain comprehensive general liability insurance and rental loss or business interruption insurance in amounts and under policies acceptable to Lender. The comprehensive general liability insurance must name Lender as
an additional insured. The rental loss or business interruption insurance must be in an amount equal to at least coverage of one year&#146;s debt service, and required escrow account deposits (if agreed to separately in writing). </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Grantor will give Lender and the insurance company immediate notice of any loss. All insurance proceeds will be applied to restoration or repair of the Property or to
the Secured Debts, at Lender&#146;s option. If Lender acquires the Property in damaged condition, Grantor&#146;s rights to any insurance policies and proceeds will pass to Lender to the extent of the Secured Debts. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Grantor will immediately notify Lender of cancellation or termination of insurance. If Grantor fails to keep the Property insured, Lender may obtain insurance to protect
Lender&#146;s interest in the Property and Grantor will pay for the insurance on Lender&#146;s demand. Lender may demand that Grantor pay for the insurance all at once, or Lender may add the insurance premiums to the balance of the Secured Debts and
charge interest on it at the rate that applies to the Secured Debts. This insurance may include coverages not originally required of Grantor, may be written by a company other than one Grantor would choose, and may be written at a higher rate than
Grantor could obtain if Grantor purchased the insurance. Grantor acknowledges and agrees that Lender or one of Lender&#146;s affiliates may receive commissions on the purchase of this insurance. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>20. ESCROW FOR TAXES AND INSURANCE. </B>Grantor will not be required to pay to Lender funds for taxes and insurance in escrow. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>21. CO-SIGNERS. </B>If Grantor signs this Security Instrument but is not otherwise obligated to pay the Secured Debts, Grantor does so only to convey Grantor&#146;s
interest in the Property to secure payment of the Secured Debts and Grantor does not agree by signing this Security Instrument to be personally liable on the Secured Debts. If this Security Instrument secures a guaranty between Lender and Grantor,
Grantor agrees to waive any rights that may prevent Lender from bringing any action or claim against Grantor or any party indebted under the obligation. These rights may include, but are not limited to, any anti-deficiency or one-action laws.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>22. SUCCESSOR TRUSTEE. </B>Lender, at Lender&#146;s option, may from time to time remove Trustee and appoint a successor or successors to any trustee
without any other formality than the designation in writing. The successor or any successors to any trustee, without conveyance of the Property, will succeed to all the title, power and duties conferred upon trustee by this Security Instrument and
applicable law. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>23. WAIVERS. </B>Except to the extent prohibited by law, Grantor waives the benefit of the homestead exemption as to
this obligation and any rights of appraisement and reinstatement. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">GRANTOR HEREBY EXPRESSLY WAIVES AND RELEASES ANY REQUIREMENT OR OBLIGATION THAT THE
LENDER OR THE TRUSTEE PRESENT EVIDENCE OR OTHERWISE PROCEED BEFORE ANY COURT, CLERK, OR OTHER JUDICIAL OR QUASI-JUDICIAL BODY BEFORE EXERCISE OF THE POWERS OF SALE CONTAINED IN THIS SECURITY INSTRUMENT AND IN SECTION 55-59 AND SECTIONS 55-59.1
THROUGH 55-59.4 OF THE CODE OF VIRGINIA (1950), AS AMENDED. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>24. APPLICABLE LAW. </B>This Security Instrument is governed by the laws of Virginia, the
United States of America, and to the extent required, by the laws of the jurisdiction where the Property is located, except to the extent such state laws are preempted by federal law. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>25. JOINT AND INDIVIDUAL LIABILITY AND SUCCESSORS. </B>Each Grantor&#146;s obligations under this Security Instrument are independent of the obligations of any other Grantor. Lender may sue each Grantor
individually or together with any other Grantor. Lender may release any part of the Property and Grantor will still be obligated under this Security Instrument for the remaining Property. Grantor agrees that Lender and any party to this Security
Instrument may extend, modify or make any change in the terms of this Security Instrument or any evidence of debt without Grantor&#146;s consent. Such a change will not release Grantor from the terms of this Security Instrument. The duties and
benefits of this Security Instrument will bind and benefit the successors and assigns of Lender and Grantor. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>26. AMENDMENT, INTEGRATION AND
SEVERABILITY. </B>This Security Instrument may not be amended or modified by oral agreement. No amendment or modification of this Security Instrument is effective unless made in writing and executed by Grantor and Lender. This Security Instrument
and any other documents relating to the Secured Debts are the complete and final expression of the agreement. If any provision of this Security Instrument is unenforceable, then the unenforceable provision will be severed and the remaining
provisions will still be enforceable. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>27. INTERPRETATION. </B>Whenever used, the singular includes the plural and the plural includes the singular. The
section headings are for convenience only and are not to be used to interpret or define the terms of this Security Instrument. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>28. NOTICE, FINANCIAL
REPORTS, ADDITIONAL DOCUMENTS AND RECORDING TAXES. </B>Unless otherwise required by law, any notice will be given by delivering it or mailing it by first class mail to the appropriate party&#146;s address listed in the DATE AND PARTIES section, or
to any other address designated in writing. Notice to one Grantor will be deemed to be notice to all Grantors. Grantor will inform Lender in writing of any change in Grantor&#146;s name, address or other application information. Grantor will provide
Lender any financial statements or information Lender requests. All financial statements and information Grantor gives Lender will be correct and complete. Grantor agrees to pay all expenses, charges and taxes in connection with the preparation and
recording of this Security Instrument. Grantor agrees to sign, deliver, and file any additional documents or certifications that Lender may consider necessary to perfect, continue, and preserve Grantor&#146;s obligations under this Security
Instrument and to confirm Lender&#146;s lien status on any Property, and Grantor agrees to pay all expenses, charges and taxes in connection with the preparation and recording thereof. Time is of the essence. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>SIGNATURES. </B>By signing under seal, Grantor agrees to the terms and covenants contained in this Security Instrument. Grantor also acknowledges receipt of a copy of
this Security Instrument. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>GRANTOR:</B> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:8%; text-indent:4%"><FONT

FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(Commercial - Draw) </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>DATE AND PARTIES. </B>The date of this Promissory Note (Note) is September&nbsp;22, 2006. The
parties and their addresses are: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>LENDER:</B> </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>VALLEY BANK</B> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"

STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Telephone: (540)&nbsp;342-2265 </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2"><B>BORROWER:</B> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>OPTICAL CABLE CORPORATION</B> </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">a Virginia Corporation </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">5290 Concourse Drive </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Roanoke, Virginia 24019 </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>1. DEFINITIONS. </B>As used in this Note, the terms have the following meanings: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A. Pronouns. </B>The pronouns &#147;I,&#148; &#147;me,&#148; and &#147;my&#148; refer to each Borrower signing this Note, individually and together. &#147;You&#148; and &#147;Your&#148; refer to the Lender.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>B. Note. </B>Note refers to this document, and any extensions, renewals, modifications and substitutions of this Note. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>C. Loan. </B>Loan refers to this transaction generally, including obligations and duties arising from the terms of all documents prepared or submitted
for this transaction such as applications, security agreements, disclosures or notes, and this Note. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>D. Loan Documents. </B>Loan
Documents refer to all the documents executed as a part of or in connection with the Loan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>E. Property. </B>Property is any property,
real, personal or intangible, that secures my performance of the obligations of this Loan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>F. Percent. </B>Rates and rate change
limitations are expressed as annualized percentages. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>2. PROMISE TO PAY. </B>For value received, I promise to pay you or your order, at your address, or
at such other location as you may designate, amounts advanced from time to time under the terms of this Note up to the maximum total principal balance of <B>$6,500,000.00 (Principal)</B>, plus interest from the date of disbursement, on the unpaid
outstanding Principal balance until this Note is paid in full and Lender has no further obligations to make advances to you under this Loan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">All advances
made will be made subject to all other terms and conditions of this Loan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>3. INTEREST. </B>Interest will accrue on the unpaid Principal balance of this
Note during the first phase of the Loan at the rate of <B>7.5 percent (Interest Rate) </B>until October&nbsp;1, 2007. After which time, interest will accrue on the unpaid Principal balance during the second phase of the Loan at a rate of 7.5
percent. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A. Interest After Default. </B>If a default occurs under the terms of this Loan, including for failure to pay in full at
maturity, you may increase the Interest Rate payable on the outstanding Principal balance of this Note. In such event, interest will accrue on the outstanding Principal balance at the Interest Rate in effect from time to time under the terms of this
Loan, until paid in full. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>B. Maximum Interest Amount. </B>Any amount assessed or collected as interest under the terms of this Note will
be limited to the maximum lawful amount of interest allowed by state or federal law, whichever is greater. Amounts collected in excess of the maximum lawful amount will be applied first to the unpaid Principal balance. Any remainder will be refunded
to me. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>C. Statutory Authority. </B>The amount assessed or collected on this Note is authorized by the Virginia usury laws under Va. Code
&#167;&#167; 6.1-330.49 et. seq. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>D. Accrual. </B>Interest accrues using an Actual/360 days counting method. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>4. ADDITIONAL CHARGES. </B>As additional consideration, I agree to pay, or have paid, these additional fees and charges. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A. Nonrefundable Fees and Charges. </B>The following fees are earned when collected and will not be
refunded if I prepay this Note before the scheduled maturity date. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:8%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Loan Origination. </B>A(n) Loan Origination fee of $32,500.00 payable
from separate funds on or before today&#146;s date. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:8%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Flood Certification. </B>A(n) Flood Certification fee of $25.00 payable from
separate funds on or before today&#146;s date. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>5. REMEDIAL CHARGES. </B>In addition to interest or other finance charges, I agree that I will pay these
additional fees based on my method and pattern of payment. Additional remedial charges may be described elsewhere in this Note. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A. Late
Charge. </B>If a payment is more than <B>7 </B>days late, I will be charged <B>5.000 </B>percent of the Unpaid Portion of Payment. I will pay this late charge promptly but only once for each late payment. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>B. Returned Check Charge. </B>I agree to pay a fee not to exceed $29.00 for each check, negotiable order of withdrawal or draft I issue in connection
with this Loan that is returned because it has been dishonored. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>C. Trustee Fee. </B>A(n) Trustee Fee equal to 5.000 percent of the
Balance of the Loan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>6. GOVERNING AGREEMENT. </B>This Note is further governed by the Commercial Loan Agreement executed between you and me as a part
of this Loan, as modified, amended or supplemented. The Commercial Loan Agreement states the terms and conditions of this Note, including the terms and conditions under which the maturity of this Note may be accelerated. When I sign this Note, I
represent to you that I have reviewed and am in compliance with the terms contained in the Commercial Loan Agreement. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>7. PAYMENT. </B>I agree to pay
this Note in <B>60 </B>installment payments. During the first phase of the Loan I will make <B>12 </B>payments of accrued interest beginning November&nbsp;1, 2006, and then on the 1st day of each month thereafter, until October&nbsp;1, 2007.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Then, I agree to make <B>48 </B>installment payments during the second phase of the Loan. The second phase of this Note is amortized over <B>300
</B>payments. I will make <B>47 </B>payments of <B>$48,501.60 </B>beginning on November&nbsp;1, 2007, and on the 1st day of each month thereafter. A single &#147;balloon payment&#148; of the entire unpaid balance of Principal and interest will be
due October&nbsp;1, 2011. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Payments will be rounded to the nearest $.01. With the final payment I also agree to pay any additional fees or charges owing
and the amount of any advances you have made to others on my behalf. Payments scheduled to be paid on the 29th, 30th or 31st day of a month that contains no such day will, instead, be made on the last day of such month. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Each payment I make on this Note will be applied first to interest that is due then to principal that is due, and finally to any charges that I owe other than principal
and interest. If you and I agree to a different application of payments, we will describe our agreement on this Note. You may change how payments are applied in your sole discretion without notice to me. The actual amount of my final payment will
depend on my payment record. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>8. PREPAYMENT. </B>I may prepay this Loan in full or in part at any time. Any partial prepayment will not excuse any later
scheduled payments until I pay in full. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>9. LOAN PURPOSE. </B>The purpose of this Loan is to fund future acquisitions and investments. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>10. ADDITIONAL TERMS. </B>This note is cross collateralized and cross defaulted with note numbers 156809&nbsp;&amp; 156833. </FONT></P> <P
